<rate>2< /rate>< text>
This review is not based on the knowledge of the vet, but on the service and overall care. I will give the pros and con of my experience.
Pros: easy to get appointments, even at last minute for emergencies (within business hours). Staff is pleasant. Prices are comparable. Patient and willing to answer many questions
Cons: poor communication. Almost zero follow up. Vague diagnostics, need to probe to get a thorough understanding of findings.
One of my experiences: They agreed to see my cat without apps. on a Monday. He had been vomiting all weekend and stopped eating Sunday. I got a call early afternoon saying they needed to do blood work and x-rays. I agreed to x-rays, and if they couldn't find the problem to do the blood work.
After x-rays I was told by he appeared to have swelling of the pancreas, diagnosis pancreatitis.
When I went to pick him up, they told me to come at 5 which is closing time, the Dr. came out and reaffirmed the diagnosis. He explained the medicine he was giving me would be for inflammation and one for appetite. He said there would be one for vomiting, but then after I ask for clarification of administering the meds., he said there were 2 and one of them would help with the vomiting. I had to ask a bunch of questions about why he thought it was pancreatitis and not a blockage or diabetes or something else. He didn't explain the seriousness of the diagnosis At all.
The next day, my cat was still not eating, it was the 3rd day without food. My research said it is very serious if cats don't eat after 3 days. I called the vet wanting to know what I was really dealing with. I wanted to know if I was going to have to euthanize as he was rapidly declining and I had found out from personal research how serious this was. I spoke to a tech who was very nice, calmed me down and said to just relax and be with my cat and not project stress on him, but to just be comforting. The vet would call me back later. He did not call back.
I called again the next day, day 4 of my cat not eating. He was now just lying on the floor looking like road kill. Vet finally called me later that day. Just before he did, my cat had finally had something to eat. I continued all meds. and he got back to normal. After that last call I had no follow up from the vet.
Forward to 5 weeks later, my cat starts vomiting and crying again. I call the vet right when office opens to see what I should do. The receptionist says vet will call later that afternoon, or by 5. At 5 I called back ND was told I was 3rd on the call back list. He NEVER called me back. This is a serious life threatening chronic problem my cat is having and his vet is doing NOTHING!
This is just one experience. The vet handed lacerations on my other cat great, but then gave me antibiotics for another cat that had hair loss on his nose and said "let's see if this works" basically didn't know what it was but if the meds. worked it meant it was an infection.
Hope this gives you enough info. to make an informed decision.< /text>

<text>As long as they retain their current manager, I will not be eating at or ordering from here.
This is a regular favorite for me and I recently placed a to go order where I requested their corn tortillas (as I mentioned previously, the handmade tortillas here are a highlight). When I arrived, I found they had substituted in cheap, store bought tortillas on my tacos. Previously my waiters had only ever mentioned that the restaurant had 2 types of tortillas (flour and handmade corn), so I was confused, and asked why this had occurred. Apparently their new policy (which is written nowhere), is that you need to include the word "Handmade" with the request for "Corn tortillas" in the ordering instructions box. I asked what I would need to pay I would need to pay to have the order switched over to the handmade tortillas (this was really the only reason I had chosen to order from here). The manager (a large woman with an Eastern Bloc accent) refused to remake my order or told me they'd need to recharge me for the entire order (including the cost of the appetizers and sides). She insisted I could purchase handmade corn tortillas and just "flip" the contents of the taco over myself at home. Sounds fine, but 1. I don't want to assemble tacos at home. That's why I'm ordering takeout. 2. I ended up having to do this and the tacos were super dry because none of the sauce is retained when you "flip" them, and 3. How hard is it to just "flip" the tacos yourself for a customer and add a little more sauce? After much back and forth with this extremely rude and condescending woman, she eventually gave me some tortillas, and I was left with dry tacos that needed to be assembled at home (as mentioned above).
Note to Owner: It would be much easier to revise your online menu to allow customers to select tortilla options than to berate your loyal customers in order to enforce unannounced policy changes.
I've been a regular here since they opened and have recommended it to a ton of friends. The food is great. But after this experience, I will not be back. I can't imagine how awful this woman would be if you had a food allergy.
We have a lot of choices in which restaurants to support in coming out of this pandemic. This will not be one of them.<//text><Pics>None< /Pics>< Response>

My go to favorite San Bruno Avenue tea house was unexpectedly closed üò± so I decided to try a neighboring tea house Tea Plus! Firstly, their happy hour special is a few cents cheaper than my fav place which was a instant plus in these penny pinching pandemic times! I ordered a Passion Fruit Slushy with a combination of passion fruit jellies and bobas and while not as photogenic as my favorite drink it was absolutely delish, I was munching on jellies and bobas for awhile after the drink was finished so it's safe to say the ordering of the extra combo probably was overkill. The one truly wonderful part of my visit to Tea Plus was the customer service. The older gentleman that was supervising a younger worker took over as I think my add-ons were a bit complicated to the check out app they used and he was friendly and knowledgeable and made me feel very welcome I felt that my drink choice was in truly good hands. Customer service is a rarity around SF at most times so when it is provided I'm always apppreciative! The cons would be that the ambiance is lacking and the drinks again aren't very photogenic but the pros heavily outweigh these small cons. Five star customer service and a yummy in my tummy afternoon drink! Thank you Tea Plus I will be visiting again for sure and now I have two very favorite San Bruno Avenue Tea Houses for my special treats! I think next time I'll be trying the crepes as well or maybe even the spam hand roll! *** Major plus I didn't pay an upcharge for my jelly boba combos!< /review>

<rating>4< /rating>< review>
So, I‚Äôve never been to a ‚ÄúEscape Room‚Äù and heard people talk about it and post about it. But now I did and I can talk about it! Hahaha.

The facility - 4 stars: If you haven‚Äôt been there, it was confusing to know and see where the entrance was. The Red Door is actually on the second floor. The facility itself is nice. The downstairs portion looks like ‚Äúit‚Äôs community‚Äù meaning not necessarily for the Red Door Escape Room but you can use it. There‚Äôs a restrooms available downstairs and one upstairs in the vicinity of the Escape Room. The facility was nice and clean.

The Game - 5 stars: The game we chose was ‚ÄúCash Me if You Can‚Äù the room was tiny but enough for seven people. Don‚Äôt know how the other rooms are since this was my first time. The game was pretty fun and challenging. It really requires brain power and communication. The set up is awesome and so are the props. They are things we would use in real life, no fake props. If you‚Äôre up for a challenge choose this game. This game is good for ages 7 and up as long as the young ones are with parents. I think this would also be good for a party or for out of towner visitors!!! I love the concept of no phones inside! I will be back to do other games!!!

The staff 5 stars: very nice, very helpful, and had smiles on their faces. What more can I say? And after we did our escape, they were willing to answer questions! Great job staff!!!< /review>

Had a really fun experience here. Planned it for a group of friends and we had a blast. The front team and our helper were great. My only complaint is that when you book ahead, it isn‚Äôt convenient and the ability to get a refund doesn‚Äôt exist. So I booked a room that could hold 12 but we only had 9 people and so I booked and paid the extra so that it could just be our group. But I was worried to book because our 9 th person was iffy because she had surgery recently and wasn‚Äôt sure she would feel up to it. I decided to book anyway and stop delaying as I was afraid it would book up. She finally decided to bow out which was fine and I called and they let me switch to an eight person game. I expected a refund for the $40 additional I had paid since we switched games, but the worker was only allowed to give me a store credit. Her answer was simply, ‚ÄúThe policy is we don‚Äôt do any refunds.‚Äù I am sorry, but that is ridiculous. They must be afraid of the merchant fee that comes from a return. Now I am stuck with $40 credit and a bad taste. I am not going to go an ask my friend who just had surgery to buy it off me as that would be rude and inconsiderate. < Review>
We did the Prison Break room with 5 experienced escapers and 1 noob. It was a decent room, all equipment in solid working order. Staff was friendly and attentive even though the place was really busy. We escaped in 27 minutes (supposedly 2nd place for the room) so it was decidedly on the easier side. Probably really good for people who haven't been before or who have only done one or two rooms. Definitely will get you grounded in the concepts without being unescapable for new people.</Review>
